\doxysection{Duin\+Maths.\+h}
\hypertarget{_duin_maths_8h_source}{}\label{_duin_maths_8h_source}\index{Duin/src/Duin/Core/Maths/DuinMaths.h@{Duin/src/Duin/Core/Maths/DuinMaths.h}}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{00001\ \textcolor{comment}{/**********************************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00002\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00003\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ raymath\ v2.0\ -\/\ Math\ functions\ to\ work\ with\ Vector2,\ Vector3,\ Matrix\ and\ Quaternions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00004\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00005\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ CONVENTIONS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Matrix\ structure\ is\ defined\ as\ row-\/major\ (memory\ layout)\ but\ parameters\ naming\ AND\ all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ math\ operations\ performed\ by\ the\ library\ consider\ the\ structure\ as\ it\ was\ column-\/major}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ It\ is\ like\ transposed\ versions\ of\ the\ matrices\ are\ used\ for\ all\ the\ maths}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ It\ benefits\ some\ functions\ making\ them\ cache-\/friendly\ and\ also\ avoids\ matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ transpositions\ sometimes\ required\ by\ OpenGL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Example:\ In\ memory\ order,\ row0\ is\ [m0\ m4\ m8\ m12]\ but\ in\ semantic\ math\ row0\ is\ [m0\ m1\ m2\ m3]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Functions\ are\ always\ self-\/contained,\ no\ function\ use\ another\ raymath\ function\ inside,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ required\ code\ is\ directly\ re-\/implemented\ inside}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Functions\ input\ parameters\ are\ always\ received\ by\ value\ (2\ unavoidable\ exceptions)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Functions\ use\ always\ a\ "{}result"{}\ variable\ for\ return\ (except\ C++\ operators)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Functions\ are\ always\ defined\ inline}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Angles\ are\ always\ in\ radians\ (DEG2RAD/RAD2DEG\ macros\ provided\ for\ convenience)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ No\ compound\ literals\ used\ to\ make\ sure\ libray\ is\ compatible\ with\ C++}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ CONFIGURATION:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RAYMATH\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Generates\ the\ implementation\ of\ the\ library\ into\ the\ included\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ If\ not\ defined,\ the\ library\ is\ in\ header\ only\ mode\ and\ can\ be\ included\ in\ other\ headers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ or\ source\ files\ without\ problems.\ But\ only\ ONE\ file\ should\ hold\ the\ implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RAYMATH\_STATIC\_INLINE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Define\ static\ inline\ functions\ code,\ so\ \#include\ header\ suffices\ for\ use.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ This\ may\ use\ up\ lots\ of\ memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RAYMATH\_DISABLE\_CPP\_OPERATORS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Disables\ C++\ operator\ overloads\ for\ raymath\ types.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00410\ DNMAPI\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ FastSqrt(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ x)\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00411\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00412\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ !defined(EPSILON)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00413\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \ \ \#define\ EPSILON\ 0.000001f}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00414\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00415\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ result\ =\ 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00416\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (fabs(x)\ <=\ EPSILON)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00417\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00418\ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00419\ \ \ \ \ \_\_m128\ input\ =\ \_mm\_set\_ss(x);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00420\ \ \ \ \ \_\_m128\ rsqrt\ =\ \_mm\_rsqrt\_ss(input);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00421\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00422\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Perform\ one\ iteration\ of\ Newton-\/Raphson\ to\ refine\ the\ result:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00423\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ rsqrt\ =\ rsqrt\ *\ (1.5\ -\/\ 0.5\ *\ x\ *\ rsqrt\ *\ rsqrt);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00424\ \ \ \ \ \_\_m128\ half\ =\ \_mm\_set\_ss(0.5f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00425\ \ \ \ \ \_\_m128\ three\ =\ \_mm\_set\_ss(1.5f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00426\ \ \ \ \ \_\_m128\ refined\ =\ \_mm\_mul\_ss(rsqrt,\ \_mm\_sub\_ss(three,\ \_mm\_mul\_ss(half,\ \_mm\_mul\_ss(input,\ \_mm\_mul\_ss(rsqrt,\ rsqrt)))));}
\DoxyCodeLine{00427\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00428\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Multiply\ the\ refined\ reciprocal\ square\ root\ by\ x\ to\ get\ sqrt(x)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00429\ \ \ \ \ \_\_m128\ sqrt\ =\ \_mm\_mul\_ss(input,\ refined);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00430\ \ \ \ \ result\ =\ \_mm\_cvtss\_f32(sqrt);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00431\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00432\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00433\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00434\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{00545\ DNMAPI\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ Vector2Angle(Vector2\ v1,\ Vector2\ v2)}

\DoxyCodeLine{00709\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Move\ Vector\ towards\ target}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00710\ DNMAPI\ Vector2\ Vector2MoveTowards(Vector2\ v,\ Vector2\ target,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ maxDistance)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00711\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00712\ \ \ \ \ Vector2\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00713\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00714\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ dx\ =\ target.x\ -\/\ v.x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00715\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ dy\ =\ target.y\ -\/\ v.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00716\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ value\ =\ (dx*dx)\ +\ (dy*dy);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00717\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00718\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ ((value\ ==\ 0)\ ||\ ((maxDistance\ >=\ 0)\ \&\&\ (value\ <=\ maxDistance*maxDistance)))\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ target;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00719\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00720\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ dist\ =\ sqrtf(value);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00721\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00722\ \ \ \ \ result.x\ =\ v.x\ +\ dx/dist*maxDistance;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00723\ \ \ \ \ result.y\ =\ v.y\ +\ dy/dist*maxDistance;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00724\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00725\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00726\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00727\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00728\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Move\ Vector\ towards\ target\ using\ FastSqrt}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00734\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ dy\ =\ target.y\ -\/\ v.y;}

\DoxyCodeLine{00767\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Clamp\ the\ magnitude\ of\ the\ vector\ between\ two\ min\ and\ max\ values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00768\ DNMAPI\ Vector2\ Vector2ClampValue(Vector2\ v,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ min,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ max)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00769\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00770\ \ \ \ \ Vector2\ result\ =\ v;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00771\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00772\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ length\ =\ (v.x*v.x)\ +\ (v.y*v.y);}

\DoxyCodeLine{00776\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00777\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ scale\ =\ 1;\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ By\ default,\ 1\ as\ the\ neutral\ element.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00778\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (length\ <\ min)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00779\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00780\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ scale\ =\ min/length;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00781\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00851\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{00859\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ v.y\ =\ r*v.y\ -\/\ (r*dot\ +\ d)*n.y;}

\DoxyCodeLine{01340\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Move\ Vector\ towards\ target}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01341\ DNMAPI\ Vector3\ Vector3MoveTowards(Vector3\ v,\ Vector3\ target,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ maxDistance)}
\DoxyCodeLine{01342\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{01343\ \ \ \ \ Vector3\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01344\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01345\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ dx\ =\ target.x\ -\/\ v.x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01346\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ dy\ =\ target.y\ -\/\ v.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01347\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ dz\ =\ target.z\ -\/\ v.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01348\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ value\ =\ (dx*dx)\ +\ (dy*dy)\ +\ (dz*dz);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01349\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01350\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ ((value\ ==\ 0)\ ||\ ((maxDistance\ >=\ 0)\ \&\&\ (value\ <=\ maxDistance*maxDistance)))\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ target;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01351\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01352\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ dist\ =\ sqrtf(value);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01353\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01354\ \ \ \ \ result.x\ =\ v.x\ +\ dx/dist*maxDistance;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01355\ \ \ \ \ result.y\ =\ v.y\ +\ dy/dist*maxDistance;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01356\ \ \ \ \ result.z\ =\ v.z\ +\ dz/dist*maxDistance;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01357\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01358\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01359\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01360\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01361\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Move\ Vector\ towards\ target\ using\ FastSqrt}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01362\ DNMAPI\ Vector3\ Vector3MoveTowardsF(Vector3\ v,\ Vector3\ target,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ maxDistance)}
\DoxyCodeLine{01363\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{01364\ \ \ \ \ Vector3\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01365\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01366\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ dx\ =\ target.x\ -\/\ v.x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01367\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ dy\ =\ target.y\ -\/\ v.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01368\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ dz\ =\ target.z\ -\/\ v.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01369\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ value\ =\ (dx*dx)\ +\ (dy*dy)\ +\ (dz*dz);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01370\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01371\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ ((value\ ==\ 0)\ ||\ ((maxDistance\ >=\ 0)\ \&\&\ (value\ <=\ maxDistance*maxDistance)))\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ target;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01372\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01373\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ dist\ =\ FastSqrt(value);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01374\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01375\ \ \ \ \ result.x\ =\ v.x\ +\ dx/dist*maxDistance;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01376\ \ \ \ \ result.y\ =\ v.y\ +\ dy/dist*maxDistance;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01377\ \ \ \ \ result.z\ =\ v.z\ +\ dz/dist*maxDistance;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01378\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01379\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01380\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01381\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01382\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Calculate\ linear\ interpolation\ between\ two\ vectors}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01384\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{01385\ \ \ \ \ Vector3\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01386\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01387\ \ \ \ \ result.x\ =\ v1.x\ +\ amount*(v2.x\ -\/\ v1.x);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01388\ \ \ \ \ result.y\ =\ v1.y\ +\ amount*(v2.y\ -\/\ v1.y);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01389\ \ \ \ \ result.z\ =\ v1.z\ +\ amount*(v2.z\ -\/\ v1.z);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01390\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01391\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01392\ \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01394\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Calculate\ cubic\ hermite\ interpolation\ between\ two\ vectors\ and\ their\ tangents}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01395\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ as\ described\ in\ the\ GLTF\ 2.0\ specification:\ https://registry.khronos.org/glTF/specs/2.0/glTF-\/2.0.html\#interpolation-\/cubic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01396\ DNMAPI\ Vector3\ Vector3CubicHermite(Vector3\ v1,\ Vector3\ tangent1,\ Vector3\ v2,\ Vector3\ tangent2,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ amount)}
\DoxyCodeLine{01397\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{01398\ \ \ \ \ Vector3\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01399\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01400\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ amountPow2\ =\ amount*amount;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01401\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ amountPow3\ =\ amount*amount*amount;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01402\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01403\ \ \ \ \ result.x\ =\ (2*amountPow3\ -\/\ 3*amountPow2\ +\ 1)*v1.x\ +\ (amountPow3\ -\/\ 2*amountPow2\ +\ amount)*tangent1.x\ +\ (-\/2*amountPow3\ +\ 3*amountPow2)*v2.x\ +\ (amountPow3\ -\/\ amountPow2)*tangent2.x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01404\ \ \ \ \ result.y\ =\ (2*amountPow3\ -\/\ 3*amountPow2\ +\ 1)*v1.y\ +\ (amountPow3\ -\/\ 2*amountPow2\ +\ amount)*tangent1.y\ +\ (-\/2*amountPow3\ +\ 3*amountPow2)*v2.y\ +\ (amountPow3\ -\/\ amountPow2)*tangent2.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01405\ \ \ \ \ result.z\ =\ (2*amountPow3\ -\/\ 3*amountPow2\ +\ 1)*v1.z\ +\ (amountPow3\ -\/\ 2*amountPow2\ +\ amount)*tangent1.z\ +\ (-\/2*amountPow3\ +\ 3*amountPow2)*v2.z\ +\ (amountPow3\ -\/\ amountPow2)*tangent2.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01406\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01407\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01408\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01409\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01410\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Calculate\ reflected\ vector\ to\ normal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01411\ DNMAPI\ Vector3\ Vector3Reflect(Vector3\ v,\ Vector3\ normal)}
\DoxyCodeLine{01412\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{01413\ \ \ \ \ Vector3\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01414\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01415\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ I\ is\ the\ original\ vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01416\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ N\ is\ the\ normal\ of\ the\ incident\ plane}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01417\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ R\ =\ I\ -\/\ (2*N*(DotProduct[I,\ N]))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01418\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01419\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ dotProduct\ =\ (v.x*normal.x\ +\ v.y*normal.y\ +\ v.z*normal.z);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01420\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01421\ \ \ \ \ result.x\ =\ v.x\ -\/\ (2.0f*normal.x)*dotProduct;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01422\ \ \ \ \ result.y\ =\ v.y\ -\/\ (2.0f*normal.y)*dotProduct;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01423\ \ \ \ \ result.z\ =\ v.z\ -\/\ (2.0f*normal.z)*dotProduct;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01424\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01425\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01426\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01427\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{01465\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ d21\ =\ (v2.x*v1.x\ +\ v2.y*v1.y\ +\ v2.z*v1.z);\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Vector3DotProduct(v2,\ v1)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01938\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Move\ Vector\ towards\ target}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01939\ DNMAPI\ Vector4\ Vector4MoveTowards(Vector4\ v,\ Vector4\ target,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ maxDistance)}
\DoxyCodeLine{01940\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{01941\ \ \ \ \ Vector4\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01942\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01943\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ dx\ =\ target.x\ -\/\ v.x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01944\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ dy\ =\ target.y\ -\/\ v.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01945\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ dz\ =\ target.z\ -\/\ v.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01946\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ dw\ =\ target.w\ -\/\ v.w;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01947\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ value\ =\ (dx*dx)\ +\ (dy*dy)\ +\ (dz*dz)\ +\ (dw*dw);}

\DoxyCodeLine{01951\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ dist\ =\ sqrtf(value);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01952\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{01954\ \ \ \ \ result.y\ =\ v.y\ +\ dy/dist*maxDistance;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01955\ \ \ \ \ result.z\ =\ v.z\ +\ dz/dist*maxDistance;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01956\ \ \ \ \ result.w\ =\ v.w\ +\ dw/dist*maxDistance;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01957\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01958\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01959\ \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02173\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ NOTE:\ When\ multiplying\ matrices...\ the\ order\ matters!}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02209\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Create\ rotation\ matrix\ from\ axis\ and\ angle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02210\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ NOTE:\ Angle\ should\ be\ provided\ in\ radians}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02211\ DNMAPI\ Matrix\ MatrixRotate(Vector3\ axis,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ angle)}
\DoxyCodeLine{02212\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{02213\ \ \ \ \ Matrix\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02214\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02215\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ x\ =\ axis.x,\ y\ =\ axis.y,\ z\ =\ axis.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02216\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02217\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ lengthSquared\ =\ x*x\ +\ y*y\ +\ z*z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02218\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02219\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ ((lengthSquared\ !=\ 1.0f)\ \&\&\ (lengthSquared\ !=\ 0.0f))}
\DoxyCodeLine{02220\ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{02221\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ ilength\ =\ 1.0f/sqrtf(lengthSquared);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02222\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ x\ *=\ ilength;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02223\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ y\ *=\ ilength;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02224\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ z\ *=\ ilength;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02225\ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02226\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02227\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ sinres\ =\ sinf(angle);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02228\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ cosres\ =\ cosf(angle);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02229\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ t\ =\ 1.0f\ -\/\ cosres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02230\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02231\ \ \ \ \ result.m0\ =\ x*x*t\ +\ cosres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02232\ \ \ \ \ result.m1\ =\ y*x*t\ +\ z*sinres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02233\ \ \ \ \ result.m2\ =\ z*x*t\ -\/\ y*sinres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02234\ \ \ \ \ result.m3\ =\ 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02235\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02236\ \ \ \ \ result.m4\ =\ x*y*t\ -\/\ z*sinres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02237\ \ \ \ \ result.m5\ =\ y*y*t\ +\ cosres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02238\ \ \ \ \ result.m6\ =\ z*y*t\ +\ x*sinres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02239\ \ \ \ \ result.m7\ =\ 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02240\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02241\ \ \ \ \ result.m8\ =\ x*z*t\ +\ y*sinres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02242\ \ \ \ \ result.m9\ =\ y*z*t\ -\/\ x*sinres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02243\ \ \ \ \ result.m10\ =\ z*z*t\ +\ cosres;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02244\ \ \ \ \ result.m11\ =\ 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02245\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02246\ \ \ \ \ result.m12\ =\ 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02247\ \ \ \ \ result.m13\ =\ 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02248\ \ \ \ \ result.m14\ =\ 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02249\ \ \ \ \ result.m15\ =\ 1.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02250\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02251\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02252\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02253\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{02327\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ siny\ =\ sinf(-\/angle.y);}

\DoxyCodeLine{02354\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ cy\ =\ cosf(angle.y);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02355\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ sy\ =\ sinf(angle.y);}

\DoxyCodeLine{02489\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Vector3Subtract(eye,\ target)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02491\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02492\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Vector3Normalize(vz)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02493\ \ \ \ \ Vector3\ v\ =\ vz;}

\DoxyCodeLine{02499\ \ \ \ \ vz.z\ *=\ ilength;}

\DoxyCodeLine{02503\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02504\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Vector3Normalize(x)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02505\ \ \ \ \ v\ =\ vx;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02506\ \ \ \ \ length\ =\ sqrtf(v.x*v.x\ +\ v.y*v.y\ +\ v.z*v.z);}

\DoxyCodeLine{02510\ \ \ \ \ vx.y\ *=\ ilength;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02511\ \ \ \ \ vx.z\ *=\ ilength;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02512\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02513\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Vector3CrossProduct(vz,\ vx)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02515\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{02831\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Calculates\ spherical\ linear\ interpolation\ between\ two\ quaternions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02832\ DNMAPI\ Quaternion\ QuaternionSlerp(Quaternion\ q1,\ Quaternion\ q2,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ amount)}
\DoxyCodeLine{02833\ \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{02835\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02836\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ !defined(EPSILON)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02838\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02839\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02840\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ cosHalfTheta\ =\ q1.x*q2.x\ +\ q1.y*q2.y\ +\ q1.z*q2.z\ +\ q1.w*q2.w;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02841\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02842\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (cosHalfTheta\ <\ 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{02843\ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{02844\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ q2.x\ =\ -\/q2.x;\ q2.y\ =\ -\/q2.y;\ q2.z\ =\ -\/q2.z;\ q2.w\ =\ -\/q2.w;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02845\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ cosHalfTheta\ =\ -\/cosHalfTheta;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02846\ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02847\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02848\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (fabsf(cosHalfTheta)\ >=\ 1.0f)\ result\ =\ q1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02849\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (cosHalfTheta\ >\ 0.95f)\ result\ =\ QuaternionNlerp(q1,\ q2,\ amount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02850\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02851\ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{02852\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ halfTheta\ =\ acosf(cosHalfTheta);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02853\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ sinHalfTheta\ =\ sqrtf(1.0f\ -\/\ cosHalfTheta*cosHalfTheta);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02854\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02855\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (fabsf(sinHalfTheta)\ <\ EPSILON)}
\DoxyCodeLine{02856\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{02857\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ result.x\ =\ (q1.x*0.5f\ +\ q2.x*0.5f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02858\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ result.y\ =\ (q1.y*0.5f\ +\ q2.y*0.5f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02859\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ result.z\ =\ (q1.z*0.5f\ +\ q2.z*0.5f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02860\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ result.w\ =\ (q1.w*0.5f\ +\ q2.w*0.5f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02861\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02862\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02863\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{02864\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ ratioA\ =\ sinf((1\ -\/\ amount)*halfTheta)/sinHalfTheta;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02865\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ ratioB\ =\ sinf(amount*halfTheta)/sinHalfTheta;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02866\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02867\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ result.x\ =\ (q1.x*ratioA\ +\ q2.x*ratioB);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02868\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ result.y\ =\ (q1.y*ratioA\ +\ q2.y*ratioB);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02869\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ result.z\ =\ (q1.z*ratioA\ +\ q2.z*ratioB);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02870\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ result.w\ =\ (q1.w*ratioA\ +\ q2.w*ratioB);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02871\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02872\ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02873\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{02877\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Calculate\ quaternion\ cubic\ spline\ interpolation\ using\ Cubic\ Hermite\ Spline\ algorithm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02878\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ as\ described\ in\ the\ GLTF\ 2.0\ specification:\ https://registry.khronos.org/glTF/specs/2.0/glTF-\/2.0.html\#interpolation-\/cubic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02879\ DNMAPI\ Quaternion\ QuaternionCubicHermiteSpline(Quaternion\ q1,\ Quaternion\ outTangent1,\ Quaternion\ q2,\ Quaternion\ inTangent2,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ t)}
\DoxyCodeLine{02880\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{02881\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ t2\ =\ t*t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02882\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ t3\ =\ t2*t;}

\DoxyCodeLine{02890\ \ \ \ \ Quaternion\ p1\ =\ QuaternionScale(q2,\ h01);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02891\ \ \ \ \ Quaternion\ m1\ =\ QuaternionScale(inTangent2,\ h11);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02892\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02893\ \ \ \ \ Quaternion\ result;}

\DoxyCodeLine{02896\ \ \ \ \ result\ =\ QuaternionAdd(result,\ p1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02897\ \ \ \ \ result\ =\ QuaternionAdd(result,\ m1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02898\ \ \ \ \ result\ =\ QuaternionNormalize(result);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02899\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02900\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ result;}

\DoxyCodeLine{02931\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Get\ a\ quaternion\ for\ a\ given\ rotation\ matrix}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02933\ \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{03110\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Get\ the\ quaternion\ equivalent\ to\ Euler\ angles}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03111\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ NOTE:\ Rotation\ order\ is\ ZYX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03112\ DNMAPI\ Quaternion\ QuaternionFromEuler(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ pitch,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ yaw,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ roll)}
\DoxyCodeLine{03113\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{03114\ \ \ \ \ Quaternion\ result;}

\DoxyCodeLine{03118\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ y0\ =\ cosf(yaw*0.5f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{03119\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ y1\ =\ sinf(yaw*0.5f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{03120\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ z0\ =\ cosf(roll*0.5f);}

\DoxyCodeLine{03125\ \ \ \ \ result.z\ =\ x0*y0*z1\ -\/\ x1*y1*z0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03126\ \ \ \ \ result.w\ =\ x0*y0*z0\ +\ x1*y1*z1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03127\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{03128\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ result;}

\DoxyCodeLine{03131\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Get\ the\ Euler\ angles\ equivalent\ to\ quaternion\ (roll,\ pitch,\ yaw)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03132\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ NOTE:\ Angles\ are\ returned\ in\ a\ Vector3\ struct\ in\ radians}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03133\ DNMAPI\ Vector3\ QuaternionToEuler(Quaternion\ q)}
\DoxyCodeLine{03134\ \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{03137\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Roll\ (x-\/axis\ rotation)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03139\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ x1\ =\ 1.0f\ -\/\ 2.0f*(q.x*q.x\ +\ q.y*q.y);}

\DoxyCodeLine{03145\ \ \ \ \ y0\ =\ y0\ <\ -\/1.0f\ ?\ -\/1.0f\ :\ y0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03146\ \ \ \ \ result.y\ =\ asinf(y0);}

\DoxyCodeLine{03148\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Yaw\ (z-\/axis\ rotation)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03151\ \ \ \ \ result.z\ =\ atan2f(z0,\ z1);}
